 function setCookie(key, value) {
    var expires = new Date();
    expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + 24592000000); //1 year
    document.cookie = key + '=' + value + ';path=/;expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
    }
 
 function getCookie(key) {
    var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + key + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
    return keyValue ? keyValue[2] : null;
    }

      <script>
       function timeDifference(current, previous) {
     
     var msPerMinute = 60 * 1000;
     var msPerHour = msPerMinute * 60;
     var msPerDay = msPerHour * 24;
     var msPerMonth = msPerDay * 30;
     var msPerYear = msPerDay * 365;
     
     var elapsed = current - previous;
     
     if (elapsed < msPerMinute) {
          return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/1000) + ' Sekunden</b></p>';   
     }
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerHour ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Minute</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute ) + ' Minuten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerDay ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Stunde</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour ) + ' Stunden</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerMonth) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Tag</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay ) + ' Tagen</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerYear) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Monat</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth ) + ' Monaten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
     
     else {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Jahr</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear ) + ' Jahren</b></p>';   
 
 		}
  
     }
 }
 
 
 var now     = new Date(); 
 var year    = now.getFullYear();
 var month   = now.getMonth()+1; 
 var day     = now.getDate();
 var hour    = now.getHours();
 var minute  = now.getMinutes();
 
 
 var current = new Date(year, month, day, hour, minute);
      </script>

 function setCookie(key, value) {
    var expires = new Date();
    expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + 24592000000); //1 year
    document.cookie = key + '=' + value + ';path=/;expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
    }
 
 function getCookie(key) {
    var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + key + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
    return keyValue ? keyValue[2] : null;
    }

      <script>
       function timeDifference(current, previous) {
     
     var msPerMinute = 60 * 1000;
     var msPerHour = msPerMinute * 60;
     var msPerDay = msPerHour * 24;
     var msPerMonth = msPerDay * 30;
     var msPerYear = msPerDay * 365;
     
     var elapsed = current - previous;
     
     if (elapsed < msPerMinute) {
          return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/1000) + ' Sekunden</b></p>';   
     }
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerHour ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Minute</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute ) + ' Minuten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerDay ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Stunde</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour ) + ' Stunden</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerMonth) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Tag</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay ) + ' Tagen</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerYear) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Monat</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth ) + ' Monaten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
     
     else {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Jahr</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear ) + ' Jahren</b></p>';   
 
 		}
  
     }
 }
 
 
 var now     = new Date(); 
 var year    = now.getFullYear();
 var month   = now.getMonth()+1; 
 var day     = now.getDate();
 var hour    = now.getHours();
 var minute  = now.getMinutes();
 
 
 var current = new Date(year, month, day, hour, minute);
      </script>

     padding-top: 5px;
 ">

         function next() {
 	var nexturl = $('.next a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',nexturl);
 };
 
 function prev() {
 	var prevurl = $('.prev a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',prevurl);
 };
 
 $(window.document).keydown(function(e) {
 			var code = e.keyCode;
 			if (code == 37) {
                 		prev();
 			} else if (code == 39) {
 				next(); 
 			}
 });
        </script>

 function setCookie(key, value) {
    var expires = new Date();
    expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + 24592000000); //1 year
    document.cookie = key + '=' + value + ';path=/;expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
    }
 
 function getCookie(key) {
    var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + key + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
    return keyValue ? keyValue[2] : null;
    }
 
 $halfcccookie = getCookie('ad0bi');

      <script>
       function timeDifference(current, previous) {
     
     var msPerMinute = 60 * 1000;
     var msPerHour = msPerMinute * 60;
     var msPerDay = msPerHour * 24;
     var msPerMonth = msPerDay * 30;
     var msPerYear = msPerDay * 365;
     
     var elapsed = current - previous;
     
     if (elapsed < msPerMinute) {
          return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/1000) + ' Sekunden</b></p>';   
     }
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerHour ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Minute</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute ) + ' Minuten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerDay ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Stunde</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour ) + ' Stunden</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerMonth) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Tag</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay ) + ' Tagen</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerYear) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Monat</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth ) + ' Monaten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
     
     else {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Jahr</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear ) + ' Jahren</b></p>';   
 
 		}
  
     }
 }
 
 
 var now     = new Date(); 
 var year    = now.getFullYear();
 var month   = now.getMonth()+1; 
 var day     = now.getDate();
 var hour    = now.getHours();
 var minute  = now.getMinutes();
 
 
 var current = new Date(year, month, day, hour, minute);
      </script>

            <h2 style="font-size: 34px;">
             <span class="mobilehide" style="float: right; color: #fff; margin-left: 20px;">
              15.06.18
             </span>
             Habitat – Vom Mensch geprägte Lebensräume
            </h2>
            <p>
             <!--<b>Projekt</b> - -->
             Das Fotobuch »Habitat« beschäftigt sich mit den menschlichen Eingriffen in natürliche Lebensräume - von landwirtschaftlichen Flächen bis zu Straßenkreuzungen, vom Tagebau bis zu Wasserstraßen. Die Fotos sind nach übergeordneten Fragen sortiert: Wo bauen wir Rohstoffe ...

         function next() {
 	var nexturl = $('.next a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',nexturl);
 };
 
 function prev() {
 	var prevurl = $('.prev a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',prevurl);
 };
 
 $(window.document).keydown(function(e) {
 			var code = e.keyCode;
 			if (code == 37) {
                 		prev();
 			} else if (code == 39) {
 				next(); 
 			}
 });
        </script>

 function setCookie(key, value) {
    var expires = new Date();
    expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + 24592000000); //1 year
    document.cookie = key + '=' + value + ';path=/;expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
    }
 
 function getCookie(key) {
    var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + key + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
    return keyValue ? keyValue[2] : null;
    }

      <script>
       function timeDifference(current, previous) {
     
     var msPerMinute = 60 * 1000;
     var msPerHour = msPerMinute * 60;
     var msPerDay = msPerHour * 24;
     var msPerMonth = msPerDay * 30;
     var msPerYear = msPerDay * 365;
     
     var elapsed = current - previous;
     
     if (elapsed < msPerMinute) {
          return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/1000) + ' Sekunden</b></p>';   
     }
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerHour ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Minute</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute ) + ' Minuten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerDay ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Stunde</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour ) + ' Stunden</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerMonth) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Tag</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay ) + ' Tagen</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerYear) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Monat</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth ) + ' Monaten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
     
     else {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Jahr</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear ) + ' Jahren</b></p>';   
 
 		}
  
     }
 }
 
 
 var now     = new Date(); 
 var year    = now.getFullYear();
 var month   = now.getMonth()+1; 
 var day     = now.getDate();
 var hour    = now.getHours();
 var minute  = now.getMinutes();
 
 
 var current = new Date(year, month, day, hour, minute);
      </script>

         function next() {
 	var nexturl = $('.next a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',nexturl);
 };
 
 function prev() {
 	var prevurl = $('.prev a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',prevurl);
 };
 
 $(window.document).keydown(function(e) {
 			var code = e.keyCode;
 			if (code == 37) {
                 		prev();
 			} else if (code == 39) {
 				next(); 
 			}
 });
        </script>

 function setCookie(key, value) {
    var expires = new Date();
    expires.setTime(expires.getTime() + 24592000000); //1 year
    document.cookie = key + '=' + value + ';path=/;expires=' + expires.toUTCString();
    }
 
 function getCookie(key) {
    var keyValue = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + key + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
    return keyValue ? keyValue[2] : null;
    }

      <script>
       function timeDifference(current, previous) {
     
     var msPerMinute = 60 * 1000;
     var msPerHour = msPerMinute * 60;
     var msPerDay = msPerHour * 24;
     var msPerMonth = msPerDay * 30;
     var msPerYear = msPerDay * 365;
     
     var elapsed = current - previous;
     
     if (elapsed < msPerMinute) {
          return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/1000) + ' Sekunden</b></p>';   
     }
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerHour ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Minute</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMinute ) + ' Minuten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     
     else if (elapsed < msPerDay ) {
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Stunde</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerHour ) + ' Stunden</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerMonth) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p><b>Vor 1 Tag</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerDay ) + ' Tagen</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
 
     else if (elapsed < msPerYear) {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Monat</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerMonth ) + ' Monaten</b></p>';   
 
 		}
 
     }
     
     else {
 
 
 		if (Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear) == 1) {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor 1 Jahr</b></p>'; 
 
 		} else {
 
 			return '<p style="display: none;"><b>Vor ' + Math.round(elapsed/msPerYear ) + ' Jahren</b></p>';   
 
 		}
  
     }
 }
 
 
 var now     = new Date(); 
 var year    = now.getFullYear();
 var month   = now.getMonth()+1; 
 var day     = now.getDate();
 var hour    = now.getHours();
 var minute  = now.getMinutes();
 
 
 var current = new Date(year, month, day, hour, minute);
      </script>

         function next() {
 	var nexturl = $('.next a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',nexturl);
 };
 
 function prev() {
 	var prevurl = $('.prev a').attr("href");
 	$(location).attr('href',prevurl);
 };
 
 $(window.document).keydown(function(e) {
 			var code = e.keyCode;
 			if (code == 37) {
                 		prev();
 			} else if (code == 39) {
 				next(); 
 			}
 });
        </script>
